       <div class="block-content">
        <h2 class="title">
         ALL - Accor Live Limitless
        </h2>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var cookieName = $("#lang-switch").data("cookie-name");
    if (cookieName === undefined) {
        cookieName = $("#Hdev-Lang-Switch").data("cookie-name");
    }
    var hotelDevelopmentCookieName = $("#lang-switch").data("hotel-development-cookie-name");
    if (hotelDevelopmentCookieName === undefined) {
        hotelDevelopmentCookieName = $("#Hdev-Lang-Switch").data("hotel-development-cookie-name");
    }
    var CrisiscookieName = $("#lang-switch").data("Crisis-cookie-name");

    if (CrisiscookieName === undefined) {
        CrisiscookieName = "CrisisLanguage";
    }
    $(".CrisisSwitchLanguage").bind("click", function () {
        if ($(this) !== undefined) {
            var languageLocale = $(this).data("language-locale");
            var persistLanguage = $(this).data("persist-language");

            createCookie(CrisiscookieName, languageLocale, 395);

            window.location.reload();

        }
    });
    $(".language-switch-lang").bind("click", function () {
        if ($(this) !== undefined) {
            var languageLocale = $(this).data("language-locale");
            var persistLanguage = $(this).data("persist-language");

            if (persistLanguage == "True") {
                createCookie(cookieName, languageLocale, 395);
                createCookie(hotelDevelopmentCookieName, languageLocale, 395);
            } else {
                createCookie(hotelDevelopmentCookieName, languageLocale, 395);
            }

            window.location.reload();

        }
    });
    function createCookie(name, value, days) {
        if (days) {
            var date = new Date();
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + (days * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000));
            var expires = "; expires=" + date.toGMTString();
        } else var expires = "";
        document.cookie = name + "=" + value + expires + "; path=/";
        var url = window.location;
        var res = url.toString().split("/");
        var finalUrl;
        res.forEach(function (item) {
            if (item == 'en' || item == 'fr-FR') {
                finalUrl = finalUrl + '/' + value;
            } else {
                finalUrl = finalUrl + '/' + item;
            }
        });
        window.location.href.replace(finalUrl);
    }

    function readCookie(name) {
        var nameEQ = name + "=";
        var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
        for (var i = 0; i < ca.length; i++) {
            var c = ca[i];
            while (c.charAt(0) == ' ') c = c.substring(1, c.length);
            if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length, c.length);
        }
        return null;
    }

    function eraseCookie(name) {
        createCookie(name, "", -1);
    }

    $("#searchpopin").on('keyup', function (e) {
        if (e.keyCode === 13) {
            var query = $("#searchpopin").val();
            var url = $(this).closest(".popin-search").data("search-result-page-url");
            window.location.href = window.location.protocol + "//" + window.location.hostname + url + "?query=" + query;
        }
    });

    $(".search-button-popin").click(function () {
        var query = $("#searchpopin").val();
        var url = $(this).closest(".popin-search").data("search-result-page-url");
        window.location.href = window.location.protocol + "//" + window.location.hostname + url + "?query=" + query;
    });
  </script>
